               <div class="content">
                <h1 class="field__item">
                 <span class="underline">
                  Manner mag man eben.
                  <svg height="8" preserveaspectratio="none" viewbox="0 0 142 8" width="142" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
                   <path d="M0.183508888,4.58743454 C-0.532954898,4.60087029 1.49702583,6.14398049 2.06900275,6.15284237 C26.1027804,6.51675109 91.975655,4.92361416 106.275078,4.52683073 C116.220789,4.25154078 133.685788,4.43649675 141.281499,4.11832675 C143.460743,4.02656344 140.307108,1.19762335 139.251518,1.20646445 C121.805625,1.34713181 84.9149044,3.08548919 0.183508888,4.58743454 Z" fill="currentColor" transform="rotate(-.974 71.032 3.706)">
                   </path>
                  </svg>
                 </span>
                </h1>
                <div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item">
                 <p>
                  Süßwarengeschichte aus Österreich. In über 130 jähriger Familientradition werden alle Süßwaren in Österreich nach Originalrezepturen und mit besonderer Sorgfalt hergestellt. Denn Rosa macht glücklich!
                 </p>
                </div>
               </div>

           <div class="field__item">
            <div class="paragraph paragraph--type--view paragraph--view-mode--default" id="pg-213">
             <div class="field field--name-field-block field--type-block-field field--label-hidden field__item">

                 <div class="views-row teaser__layout__big">
                  <div class="views-field views-field-rendered-entity">
                   <span class="field-content">
                    <a class="teaser-link" href="/de-AT/uber-manner/abheben-mit-manner-20202021" rel="bookmark">
                     <article about="/de-AT/uber-manner/abheben-mit-manner-20202021" class="teaser__big teaser__border teaser__layout__teaser_image node node--type-page node--promoted node--sticky node--view-mode-frontpage-teaser" role="article" typeof="schema:WebPage">
                      <div class="node__content">
                       <div class="teaser-image">
                        <div class="field field--name-field-teaser-image field--type-entity-reference field--label-hidden field__item">
                         <article class="media media--type-image media--view-mode-half-width-square">
                          <div class="blazy blazy--field blazy--field-media-image blazy--field-media-image--half-width-square field field--name-field-media-image field--type-image field--label-visually_hidden" data-blazy="">

                            Image
                           </div>
                           <div class="field__item">
